# Consensus Roadmap: the status board (is X done yet?)

This file is the LIVING status board and nothing else: the authoritative "has X been built" lookup for the whole project. A question like "can people chop down trees yet?" is answered by reading this, not by asking. It is read at every session START and edited IN PLACE on STOP whenever a segment makes progress (flip a status, tombstone a done feature where it stands and point to where the work landed, deprecate or re-classify an item, or add a newly-flagged one). It is never append-only and unrelated segments are never touched. The stop-gate hook enforces this.

The prior reconciliation narrative (the headline reconciliation, Tiers A through E, the derive-from-fundamentals audit, and the dated build-history sections) moved to `docs/working/ROADMAP_REFERENCE.md`, still useful for the deeper order-of-work reasoning and the history; this file stays lean so the board never gets buried.

## Feature status board: is X done yet? (the single lookup)

This is the authoritative "has X been built" table, kept current so a question like "can people chop down trees yet?" is answered by reading this rather than by asking. Status is one of: DONE (built and proven in code), PARTIAL (some of it built, a named piece missing), GATED (built but off pending an owner calibration/decision), IN PROGRESS (being built now), NOT DONE (planned, unbuilt, with the arc that would build it). Update this on every arc that changes what is built.

**World liveliness and agency (a being acting in and on the world):**
- IN PROGRESS (seam 4, the deep-time run, task #69, branch claude/seam4-deeptime): SLICE 1 LANDED (sim/deeptime.rs, dormant, byte-neutral): DeepTimeState (a lateral field of interior mantle columns + the elapsed-Myr clock) + step_deep_time, which steps each column's convection (the built convection_step) each tick so the interior cools/convects over deep time and LATERAL VARIATION emerges (a fresh planet starts uniform; columns with different radiogenic heat diverge into provinces, the written record of each column's history, never an authored map). 4 tests (evolves-over-deep-time, provinces-emerge, deterministic, fail-loud). SLICE 2 LANDED (volcanism): DeepTimeState gains crust_thickness_km (per column) + MeltParams + crust_growth, which drives each column's interior temperature through the seam-6 adiabatic_melt_column (McKenzie-Bickle) and grows the crust it delivers over the deep-time history TOWARD each column's melt-column equilibrium and SATURATES there (the finite fusible source depletes; a made crust stays and does not un-form; a sub-solidus column builds none), so the crust spread is bounded, never an unbounded integral. So the derived crustal thickness is the integrated melt history, hot columns building thicker crust (the provinces in relief) = the mechanism that RETIRES the 30km literal. 6 tests. Reserved-with-basis: the mantle processing time (overturn/melt-delivery timescale ~100Myr-1Gyr). SLICE 3 LANDED (star aging, 225310b): the star BRIGHTENS on the same deep-time clock: DeepTimeState gains star_age_start_myr, stellar_luminosity_ratio(age) = L_zams/(1 - c*t/t_ms) (Gough 1981), with t_ms = t_sun*(M/M_sun)/(L_zams/L_sun) the derived nuclear lifetime (a heavier star leaves faster since L~M^3.5); ZAMS anchor recovered at age 0, caps to None past t_ms (post-MS = #77). Reserved-with-basis + cited: t_sun ~10Gyr (Kippenhahn-Weigert), c~0.4 (Gough 1981, the faint-young-Sun ~30-40%), carried as per-star StarAgingParams data. 14 deeptime tests, both pins hold. VIEWER POLISH (owner run feedback 2026-07-15): the STAR SIZE now DERIVES from its apparent angular diameter (star_radius_ratio threaded out of derive_planet -> the scene; on-screen star_r = base * radius_ratio/orbit_au relative to the Sun-at-1-AU reference), so a big or close star draws large and a small or far one small (a massive main-sequence star at a wide orbit is small in the sky, non-canon display projection); and the inverted up/down globe pan is fixed (Up/W now tilts toward the north). The star COLOUR was already derived (blackbody_rgb from the derived T_eff, non-canon). And the tiles-do-not-align-with-the-brightness bug is FIXED: the globe tile sample mapped the surface normal as world-up ([nx,-ny,nz]) but the Lambert lighting dotted the star direction against the screen-down normal ([nx,ny,nz]) and star_dir carried screen-down dy, so the tiles were placed in world-up y while the terminator was lit in screen-down y (a vertical-frame mismatch that also read as the inverted pan). Both now use world-up y; at IDENTITY the two sign flips cancel so the headless/living globes are byte-identical, and under a pan the terminator now tracks the tiles. All 27 viewer tests pass. SLICE 4 LANDED (impacts, impact-event composer 0c0b8d3, world/impact_event.rs): apply_impact composes the built crater law + ballistic ejecta_fan + conservative redistribute into one impact on a terrain field, carving the paraboloid bowl (the crater law's own V=(pi/8)(h/D)D^3 shape) and laying a mass-conserving ejecta blanket (delta sums to exactly 0); dormant, byte-neutral, 6 tests. DEPTH FIXTURE RETIRED (owner-caught): geodynamics::convecting_mantle_depth_m derives the convecting-mantle shell = R_planet - R_core = R_planet*(1 - cbrt(core_fraction*rho_mean/rho_core)), all capstone-derived inputs, Earth-grade ~3080km, fail-loud (core no denser than the mean -> None); the ColumnParams.depth becomes this derivation at run-path wiring (the interior MATERIAL params stay reserved -> the First Stone #79 manifest-sentinels them). REMAINING seam-4: the viewer TIME CONTROL (slice 5), HELD until the First Stone (#79) manifest-sentinels the reserved params so no fixture leaks to the run path at wiring. NEXT SLICES on the same clock: melt-driven VOLCANISM (interior T crossing the seam-6 solidus extracts melt that emplaces crust, the thickness becoming the accumulated melt = retires the 30km literal), the IMPACT CHAIN (impact_flux draw -> crater -> ejecta_fan -> redistribute), STAR AGING (main-sequence L climb), and the viewer TIME CONTROL (play/pause/step/speed) that drives it all and re-derives the surface each step. SLICE 5 LANDED (2026-07-15, viewer texture + time control, viewer-only so non-canon, both pins hold 40fe8a72.../be94e310...): the derived globe is now TEXTURED and ALIVE. The deep-time province field is wired into the viewer (`build_derived_scene` builds a lateral field of interior columns at the DERIVED province scale, steps it, and re-derives the display tiles off the accumulated per-province crust). PROVINCE SCALE DERIVES (owner's explicit catch): `deeptime::provinces_across(span, mantle_depth, cell_aspect)` = span / (mantle_depth * cell_aspect), the count around the equator and pole-to-pole from the DERIVED convecting-mantle depth (`convecting_mantle_depth_m`, retiring the depth-1 fixture, wired into the column params in megametres) over the convective cell width; the display grid (48x32) stays a viewer resolution. The per-province radiogenic budget is the thermostat base (set so the mean province's steady state sits at the solidus) times one-plus the reserved heterogeneity times a DETERMINISTIC world-seed hash (`province_seed_perturbation`), so the provinces EMERGE from the seeded convection (zero heterogeneity gives a smooth ball, proven by test), never a painted map. Each display tile's elevation is the Airy float of its province's DERIVED crust thickness, bilinearly resampled and shaded by a continuous elevation ramp (a new opt-in `SurfaceStyle.relief_shading`), so the globe shows real topographic relief. TIME CONTROL: one non-canon `PlaybackDriver` clock (space pause, `<`/`>` or `[`/`]` slower/faster, `0` normal) governs BOTH the deep-time surface evolution on the globe (the surface visibly forms and thickens as you watch, headless-proven: a 60 Myr globe is near-smooth, a 3 Gyr globe carries strong relief) AND the planets ORBITING the sun on the system map (each at its DERIVED Kepler rate `a^-3/2`, inner faster, via `orbit::orbital_state` swept per frame; the per-world eccentricity flows to the offset ellipse with the star at the focus). Reserved-with-basis (surfaced, at their sites in `crates/viewer/src/main.rs`): the convective cell aspect (Rayleigh-Benard critical mode, sqrt(2) free-free default), the peridotite mantle solidus + slope (McKenzie-Bickle 1373 K / 130 K/GPa), the mantle processing time (~100 Myr-1 Gyr overturn), and the radiogenic heterogeneity amplitude (~0.3, mantle U/Th/K spread); the representable-scaled convection-kernel operating point is the documented units-plan interim. Honest limits: the crust magnitude is unphysical at the scaled operating point (the units-plan SI wiring is the follow-on) and grows unbounded (no crust-saturation feedback yet), so the display normalizes the relief; the run pins are untouched (viewer + dead-code substrate functions only). New tests: 2 in `deeptime.rs` (province scale + column wiring), 3 in `viewer` (seed determinism + spread, texture emerges only from a varied field, the bilinear sampler wraps + smooths). INTEGRATED onto claude/seam4-deeptime (cherry-pick f76d223, roadmap auto-merged); both pins RE-VERIFIED on the mainline branch, deeptime 16 + viewer 32 tests green, fmt clean. DERIVATION-HUNT RUNNING (owner directive 2026-07-15, "flag all reserved-with-basis for derivation checking"): all five reserved values (cell aspect, solidus + slope, processing time, heterogeneity amplitude) + the interim operating point are under an independent derive-first audit before any is accepted as reserved; the solidus is the agent's OWN flagged derive-down (the surface-composition/assemblage path from seams 5-6 should derive it from the world's endmember signature, retiring the Terran peridotite anchor and admitting an alien mantle). Findings to gate the wire-down. CELL ASPECT: `pi/a_c ~ 1.008`, the rigid-rigid eigenvalue pair consistent with `ra_crit=1708` (retiring the free-free sqrt(2)). HETEROGENEITY: Earth's 0.3 retired, now the full Shaw batch-melting enrichment `E = 1/(D + F(1-D))` over the world's own formation melt fraction F and heat-producer partition D (`heterogeneity_amplitude`), which admits the reduced-chalcophile sign flip (D>1, Wohlers-Wood) and caps the small-F blow-up; the D table is a 3a-style estimator (measured anchors + lattice-strain interpolation, fetch Blundy-Wood/Wood-Kiseeva) and the mixing efficiency is a per-system [E]-band derive-down (not universal) with a validity domain and band-propagation clause. THE FLAT DEFAULT is now named a REGIME-MARGINAL verdict (co-determined by the still-authored 1588 K Earth-MORB potential-temperature IC, the ~92 K margin inside the solidus model's own ~150 K bias), surfaced not asserted. R-YOUNG-TEMPERATURE LANDED (2026-07-16, branch worktree-agent-adb19352f7b051b84, viewer/materials/physics so non-canon, both pins hold 40fe8a72.../be94e310...): the fixed 1588 K young potential temperature is RETIRED for a melted world, decoupled from the assembly on the ATTRACTOR LICENSE as a REGIME-VERDICT slice (`crates/physics/src/young_thermal.rs`, a sibling of melting.rs). The verdict derives per world: MELTED (short-lived-radionuclide 26Al+60Fe heat on an early-formed body, or giant impacts on an Earth-mass body), NEVER-MELTED (the cold-accretion budget stays sub-solidus even at the top of the reserved energy-retention band), or MARGINAL (the band straddles the solidus, carried until the impact list resolves it). For a melted world the young potential temperature is PINNED at the magma-ocean lock-up handoff = the world's own derived solidus plus the phi_c superheat, which INVERTS the banked adiabatic_melt_column (feeding it back reproduces F = phi_c by construction), so the world re-derives super-solidus with a nonzero melt fraction, a nonzero radiogenic heterogeneity, and real relief. The DEFAULT Sun/1AU Mars-class world comes out MELTED, GAPPED (decidable now) by 26Al (SLR rise ~4460 K at the ~1 Myr isolation-mass formation time, far above its ~1680 K refractory solidus), young potential T pinned at the ~1831 K handoff, and its surface textures at ~5.0% neighbor-contrast (vs the ~2% smooth-ball floor). The mandatory SELF-TEST (`retention_band_cannot_flip_a_gapped_verdict`) is structural: the melt criterion is monotone in the retention efficiency eta, so a GAPPED verdict cannot flip across the band. Reversibility is mechanical: the reset epoch t0 (73 +/- 74 Myr, INTERIM) and the formation time are tagged interim with a scope fence to texture onset and thermal initial conditions only. Cited fetches at their sites: Ruedas 2017 (per-isotope specific heat production, DOI 10.1002/2017GC006997), Abe 1993 (phi_c, DOI 10.1029/GM074p0041) + Solomatov 2015, Hamano-Abe-Genda 2013 + Lichtenberg 2021 (the radiation-ceiling per-volatile class). The MANDATORY five-lens before-merge audit is the manager's gate. Processing time + the scaled operating point stay the SI-units derive-down. This EXPOSED that the derived relief is ~140 km, far exceeding the ~8 km crustal support bound: the deep-time crust growth (`sim/deeptime.rs`, out of this slice's scope) ACCUMULATES unphysically large relief over the aged span, which the old normalized ratio had hidden. SLICE (support-bound relief collapse) LANDED (sim/deeptime.rs, dormant, byte-neutral): relax_to_support_bound (a term applied by the caller AFTER step_deep_time, so the interior tick stays byte-identical) projects each column's Airy isostatic relief above the field datum, caps it at the DERIVED support bound sigma_y/(rho*g), and FLOWS the excess crust to the columns below the cap (the accommodation space) through the built conservative civsim_world::redistribute, so the crust bit-sum is INVARIANT (mass conserved to the bit) and every column's relief relaxes to the bound. sigma_y is DERIVED, RETIRING the reserved 1e8 Pa crustal-yield literal ON THIS PATH: derived_crust_yield_pa reads the crust's OWN operative shear strength (the Frenkel ideal G/(2*pi) scaled by the reserved-with-basis per-class knockdown, civsim_materials::properties::operative_shear_strength_gpa) and converts GPa->Pa; an illustrative 44 GPa crust at knockdown 0.015 lands sigma_y ~1.05e8 Pa and a bound ~9.79 km, of order the class-grade value the literal encoded (a cross-validation). INSTANTANEOUS-COLLAPSE idealization: the whole over-bound excess flows within the tick (a viscous flow RATE would be a reserved value, so the instantaneous limit is the derive-first floor and needs none; a rate, and a LOCAL grid-neighbour downhill flow in place of the accommodation-space fill, are the named reserved-with-basis refinements, flagged not authored). A crust denser than the mantle (k<=0) founders (a delamination regime this tall-relief collapse does not cover) and is left unchanged. 6 tests (relaxes-relief-and-conserves-mass-to-the-bit [test field: max relief 19.78->9.79 km = the bound, amplitude 20.61->10.20 km], derive-down-reads-the-crust-yield-not-the-literal, deterministic, within-bound no-op, foundering-unchanged, degenerate-soft); civsim-materials added as a sim dependency (a leaf, only the DORMANT term reads it), both run pins hold bit-exact. SLICE 5 KERNEL LANDED (2026-07-16, branch worktree-agent-a8b1088b94813403d, `crates/physics/src/flexure.rs`, DORMANT physics module so both pins hold 40fe8a72.. / be94e310..): the analytic thin-elastic-plate flexure that fills the ~100-1000 km wavelength band (mountain belts, foreland basins, volcano moats, peripheral bulges) between the convective provinces and the crater rows. Pure fixed-point functions, no run-path consumer yet (render wiring is a later slice after crater-rows lands). `flexural_rigidity` D = E T_e^3/(12(1-nu^2)) (T&S eq. 3-127 form) and `flexural_parameter` alpha = (4D/(delta_rho g))^(1/4) (T&S eq. 3-127) DERIVE the flexural wavelength: E, nu come from the banked isotropic-elastic moduli route (civsim_materials youngs_modulus_gpa/poisson_ratio over the ionic bulk modulus + Pugh shear, cited upstream), T_e/densities/g are caller inputs, no free constants (only the formula's own 12, 4, 8, 2pi, the 1/4 nested-sqrt, pi, and the Kelvin-series Euler-Mascheroni gamma). Green's functions: LINE load w(x)=(V0 alpha^3/8D)e^(-x/alpha)(cos+sin) (T&S eq. 3-130, the proven exp/cos/sin core) and POINT load w(r)=Q0(alpha^2/2pi D)kei(r/alpha) (Brotchie-Silvester 1969 / TAFI eq. 6); kei LANDED as an Abramowitz-Stegun 9.9 fixed-point ascending series (recurrence-accumulated, matches kei(1)/kei(2) to the fixed-point floor, numerical-twin + force-balance integral tests). HEADLINE conditioning proven: thin lid T_e=10km -> alpha~29.6km, thick lid T_e=40km -> alpha~83.8km from the same call (ratio 2.83 = T_e^(3/4)); zero load -> zero deflection. Unit-agnostic kernel (caller supplies one coherent system; the tests use {km, GPa, density x1000 kg/m^3, gravity km/s^2} to keep D and alpha in the Q32.32 window, since raw-SI D~1e23 overflows). 11 tests, fmt/clippy/stone0 clean. NEW STANDING RULES: any wire/connect/route ruling names what must already be BUILT; domain guards gate computation, never the vector; every distribution names its convicting population. The four provenance flags (formation era, accretion mass, bulk density, atmosphere volatiles) retire across the pipeline (stages 0-1-3, the stage-1 clock, the AIR_FIXTURE wire). The 1-m/tile creature-zoom is what the Sample(LoD) architecture buys (render the viewport patch only). SLICE 5 FLEXURE KERNEL LANDED (`92efe63`, dormant physics/flexure.rs: D, the derived flexural wavelength alpha, the line-load + point-load kei Green's functions, E/nu from the banked moduli, thin-vs-thick-lid conditioning, no free constants). MOON PRIMITIVES STANDALONE SLICE LANDED (2026-07-16, `crates/sim/src/moons.rs`, DORMANT so both pins hold 40fe8a72.. / be94e310..): the four derive-first primitives every branch of the tidal-survival filter shares, ahead of the branch wiring. `hill_radius` delegates to the proven `astro::hill_radius_au` (Earth ~0.0100 AU / ~1.5e6 km, one source of truth for the mass-ratio fold); `roche_limit` is the rigid-body form `R_planet*(2*rho_planet/rho_moon)^(1/3)` (Earth-Moon ~1.489 R_Earth) with the classical FLUID form `roche_limit_fluid` (2.44 coeff, ~2.883 R_Earth) as the documented alternative; `stable_orbit_fraction` carries the CITED Domingos-Winter-Yokoyama (2006) Hill fractions (0.4895 prograde < 0.9309 retrograde) with the eccentricity-aware `stable_orbit_fraction_ecc` + `stable_semimajor_axis` band; `tidal_recession_rate` = `3*(k2/Q)*(m/M)*(R/a)^5*n*a` in LOG-SPACE (the (R/a)^5 ~1e-9 factor never underflows Q32.32), reproducing the Earth-Moon ~3.82 cm/yr anchor (~3.73 with the round effective k2/Q). k2 (Love number) and Q (tidal quality factor) are CALLER INPUTS, reserved-with-basis at the future survival-filter call site (the planet's rigidity and dissipation, per-world: Earth effective k2~0.30/Q~12, lunar k2=0.0242/Q~38, Earth solid-body Q~280, fetch section 8), never authored in the kernel. CARD AUDIT (2026-07-16, the [alpha/Fe] card PASSED with findings, and the lesson is ONE wearing four coats: every finding is a SILENT PARAMETER, a value the representation implies but nobody chose out loud, and silence is where authorship hides from a provenance checker that audits only what was written down). (1) THE BRANCH WEIGHT `p(high-alpha | [Fe/H], epoch)` is now LOUD-INTERIM-TAGGED at its site: the levels/knee/band are fetched, the WEIGHT is this implementation's own shape, and the card's source CANNOT legally supply it (Bensby 2014 is kinematically selected to over-harvest thick-disk stars, so the morphology is selection-robust while the FRACTIONS are what the selection distorted most, by design); it needs a SEPARATE selection-corrected weight from a VOLUME-COMPLETE sample, conditioned on EPOCH (the high-alpha population is uniformly old, so a young thick-branch draw is the chemical anachronism the chain forbids). (2) sigma = 0 is not the absence of a dispersion, it is the MOST authored one (the 4.461-to-four-digits clone is that showing through, since abundance RATIOS not [Fe/H] set the condensate), so the per-branch INTRINSIC dispersion goes to fetch with its error treatment stated (total scatter ships as a tagged upper bound, never deconvolved by guesswork; the atomic-diffusion few-hundredths-dex offset in old dwarfs rides in the band, uncorrected). (3) THE BELT COUNT is not merely unfetched, it is ILL-POSED: a collisional reservoir has no total body count (it diverges toward small sizes), so the reservoir carries MASS plus a SIZE-FREQUENCY DISTRIBUTION (the Dohnanyi-lineage cascade slope is a DERIVED class result with regime breaks and the strength-to-gravity transition, conditioned on material class; the in-system convicting pair is the asteroid vs Kuiper belt) and COUNTS BECOME QUERIES WITH AN EXPLICIT SIZE FLOOR. This unifies free with two standing rulings: the crater production function was already flagged to condition on the local impactor reservoir, and this SFD IS that object (one reservoir serving impacts and belt queries). (4) LINK 2b RULED IN at zero new sources: the same Bensby DOI carries per-element Mg, Si, O rows the fetch collapsed to one alpha, so re-read it at element granularity (Mg is hydrostatic-burning alpha, Si explosive, so their ratio shifts measurably between the sequences, its own convicting test); medium priority, after the sigma and weight fetches. FETCH QUEUE: ALL FOUR CLOSED (2026-07-16). (1) The per-branch intrinsic sigma: 0.02-0.03 dex central, band 0.01-0.04, THE SAME ON BOTH BRANCHES (both discs are equally chemically tight, a finding in itself: the star-forming medium is homogeneous at the few-hundredths level regardless of enrichment era, so chemical individuality between same-environment worlds comes mostly from [Fe/H], branch, and epoch, and this sigma is the honest small remainder). Quadrature-subtracted intrinsic values, measurement error already removed. LOAD-BEARING CONDITION: these are AT FIXED AGE, so the sigma applies AFTER the epoch draw, NEVER as a marginal, or the age-slope leaks in. Extraction target: Bertran de Lis et al. 2016. (2) The branch weight: the BIMODALITY survives selection (the unselected solar-annulus map shows both sequences), so the two-branch draw STANDS and only the WEIGHT is corrupted, as ruled. The draw needs the LOCAL-VOLUME p(high-alpha|[Fe/H]) matching the declared environment. EPOCH GATES ONE-WAY: young draws are thin-branch ONLY; the weight applies within old epochs. CUBE-SPHERE + RAYON LANDED (`c5abf6f`, task #83, display-layer, both pins byte-exact): the sample cache is now the EQUI-ANGULAR CUBED SPHERE (Ronchi, Iacono & Paolucci 1996, area-equalizing, built from sin/cos/sqrt so fixed-point never needs tan; ~sqrt(2) residual face-centre-to-edge non-uniformity, the honest limit, against the lat-lon collapse to zero), 6 x 416^2 = 1,038,336 cells against the former 1440x720. The PINCH IS MEASURED, not asserted (standing test): a 10-degree polar cap held 57,600 lat-lon cells vs 5,032 at the equator (11.45x skew), and 6,740 vs 6,740 cube cells (1.00). The Sample math is UNCHANGED (same airy(crust) + crater-row stamps, only the directions re-parameterized); the living-world globe stays on LatLon and is byte-identical. RAYON parallelization folded in per the owner: re-derive 134.5 -> 39.2 ms (3.4x), tile cache 93.0 -> 28.6, lava 41.5 -> 10.6, with DETERMINISM pinned by a standing 1-thread-vs-8-thread bit-for-bit test (index-ordered collect, no shared accumulator). Honest decomposition: the parameterization ALONE is 48% slower serially (every cube cell pays an asin+atan2 to index the coarse lat-lon province field), which rayon's 4.8x more than covers; the crater stamp is ~72% of the build at the modest 40-body reservoir and scales O(cells x craters), so the parallelism matters far more when that reserved count rises. NAMED FOLLOW-ON: the per-cell (fu,fv) are run-invariant per face_res, so memoizing them retires the asin/atan2 overhead outright. TWO SEAMS the render probe caught: (a) swapping the cache alone did NOT clear the polar starburst, because the cube hillshade had kept the lat-lon east/north tangent frame, which COLLAPSES at the poles, putting the singularity back into the shading of a cache built to have none (fixed with an orthonormal tangent pair off the world axis least aligned with the normal; the tilt is basis-independent, no cos(lat) guard anywhere); (b) A FAINT POLAR WEDGE SURVIVES WITH THE HILLSHADE OFF, chased down rather than claimed away: THE SIM'S PROVINCE FIELD IS ITSELF STILL LAT-LON (15x7, columns converging at the pole), so the DISPLAY cache no longer pinches but the PHYSICS grid it resamples does. Retiring that means migrating the deep-time province field off lat-lon: RULED (2026-07-16) as SLICE 9, the planform-seeded province geometry, PROMOTED from trailing-cosmetic to LOAD-BEARING and scheduled as the NEXT SIM ARC (task #86) with a PIN-FREEZE WINDOW declared for its duration. It is the LAST surviving authored grid and the worst kind, because it authors a PREFERRED AXIS that mantle convection (effectively non-rotating at mantle viscosities) cannot know about, so the wedge is a pure coordinate artifact and every world carries the same pole-anchored tectonic structure (the same-look fixture class in geometric clothing). PIN-CULTURE CORRECTION recorded: the pins are NOT stale, they fired because this is real representation scope, so they DID THEIR JOB; the move is licensed by the re-baseline PROCEDURE existing, never by the pins being old. FIVE BINDING REQUIREMENTS: the target is the wavelength-constrained tessellation seeded from the planform draw with NO PREFERRED AXIS and resolution at the field's own derived cutoff (spherical harmonics or quasi-uniform nodes; NOT lat-lon, and NOT the display's cube-sphere, which stays DISPLAY-ONLY); representation-only so the move has one attributable cause; an equivalence bridge with invariants DECLARED FIRST (bytes may change, physics may not; the area distribution losing its latitude dependence is a sharp null); vector immutability (the pinned seeds keep their layer-4 realizations, the one new slot is the already-priced planform seed); and the pin move as an AUDITABLE pin-ledger event, not a re-bake. Does NOT block the cloud lane (assembly-side vs geodynamics-side). SLICE 6 LANDED (2026-07-16, viewer IMPACT CRATERS, viewer-only so non-canon, both pins hold 40fe8a72 / be94e310, 40 viewer tests + clippy/fmt/stone0 clean): the DERIVED planet's impact craters are now VISIBLE in the surface. step_provinces calls the built bombard_tick (sim/deeptime) alongside step_deep_time each deep-time tick (the initial DEEP_TIME_INITIAL_STEPS, playback, and rewind all route through step_provinces), so the surface accumulates its accretion-tail bombardment history (heavy early, quiescent late, the flux's own decline) into DeepTimeState::impact_relief_m on the PHYSICAL province grid, seeded on a stable per-world hash (star mass + orbit) so a world renders the same craters every run (Principle 3/10). derive_province_tiles COMPOSES the relief onto the render: elevation = airy(crust)_km + impact_relief_m/1000 (the m->km UNIT bridge, the same class of bug the hillshade slice caught), and the sun-direction hillshade shades it. ImpactFluxParams is DERIVE-FIRST: closing speed = escape velocity sqrt(2gR) from derived g,R; impactor density = the derived uncompressed bulk density; target gravity+density = derived surface gravity + crust density; ballistic cell size = circumference/pcols; ejecta speed = reserved fraction of the derived closing speed. Reserved-with-basis residues SURFACED as named constants (never inline literals): reservoir body count, sweep tau ~30 Myr, min/max impactor radius, target strength ~1e8 Pa, the competent-silicate crater coupling (Holsapple/Melosh), ejecta azimuths + step cap + per-tick cap; the Dohnanyi slope 3.5 is cited. The isostatic diagnostics (melt-texture heterogeneity + support-bound amplitude) were split onto a CRUST-ONLY tile field (derive_province_crust_tiles) so the craters do not dilute them; the bombardment is reported on its own readout (impact_count). HONEST LIMIT (surfaced): at the DERIVED ~1250-km province cells the built apply_impact deposits a sub-cell crater's full transient depth into one cell (and the crater law uses one simple-crater bowl_aspect, no complex-crater flattening), so a crater spanning a cell makes only ~degree slopes = the hillshade reads FAINTLY (~2-5/255) and a dense/large bombardment over-inflates per-cell relief; the reserved size+count are held modest, and the levers are the crater-collapse slice (flagged in impact_event.rs) and a finer impact grid decoupled from the convective province scale, never display exaggeration (owner override). SLICE (VISIBLE VOLCANISM, viewer-only, byte-neutral): the derived-planet globe now renders actively-molten provinces as a self-emitted LAVA GLOW. Per display tile the viewer bilinearly samples the province interior temperature (ColumnState.temperature) and runs the world's OWN derived-solidus melt column (adiabatic_melt_column) against it: the DERIVED melt fraction is the glow intensity (zero below the derived solidus, so solid crust does not glow) and the blackbody of that temperature (render::blackbody_rgb) is the incandescence hue (deep-red cool melt to orange-yellow hot melt). draw_globe ADDS emission*intensity to the shaded albedo (opt-in Option<&[LavaGlow]>, so the living-world/demo globes pass None and stay byte-identical), so a molten tile glows on the NIGHT side too (the emit-not-reflect giveaway). Headless --derived-globe across epochs shows the arc: a young world glows broadly (Sun/1AU at 0 ticks reads 100% molten, mean melt-glow 0.40), and it fades as the deep-time clock cools it to a steady state of ~48% super-solidus hot-spots (mean ~0.09) on mostly-solid crust. No authored glow threshold (the DERIVED solidus is the only cutoff); the one display constant is LAVA_EMISSION_GAIN (a non-canon emission brightness, a sibling of AMBIENT, anchored so the ~0.4 rheological-lock-up melt fraction emits at ~full brightness). Both pins hold (40fe8a72.., be94e310..); fmt/clippy clean; 2 new tests (glow fades as the world cools, a sub-solidus world does not glow). ANALYTIC NORMALS LANDED (2026-07-16, the render-strategy build-order item #1, viewer-only so both pins hold 40fe8a72.. / be94e310..): the hillshade normal is now the ANALYTIC GRADIENT of the Sample superposition rather than a finite difference of the sample cache. `render::SurfaceField` is the Sample in one place (`height_km` = airy(province crust) + crater-row stamps, the function the cube cache memoizes; `gradient` = the same superposition differentiated layer by layer), so the heights and the normals cannot drift apart: the province layer contributes the Airy buoyant fraction times the bilinear interpolant's exact gradient carried into the east/north frame through the body radius, and each crater row contributes its own crater-law derivative in rim-radii (the excavation paraboloid's `df/dx = 2 h x` inside the rim, the McGetchin blanket's `df/dx = -3h/(4 x^4)` outside), chain-ruled to arc length and pointing along the great circle away from the crater. No baking, no finite differencing, evaluated at query time; the living-world globe passes no field and keeps the cache difference, byte-identical. THE NUMERICAL TWIN (the standing rule) is the gate: the analytic gradient is differenced against the SAME Sample over a step sweep and shows the central difference's SECOND-ORDER convergence (measured mean order 1.99, error ratios 3.84/3.97/3.98/4.11 as h halves) on the crater EJECTA BLANKET, which is the only layer with a non-vanishing third derivative: the excavation bowl is EXACTLY quadratic in x so its central difference is exact (residual at the ~4e-7 fixed-point floor, no rate to measure), and the province layer's twin is floored by a 1/4096 quantization of the pre-existing lerp weight (`PROVINCE_LERP_STEPS`), so it wants a COARSE step (2.4e-7 at h=5e-2) and degrades to noise below it, the opposite of the usual story. Each layer is therefore twinned in its OWN measured window, and the composed Sample in their overlap. VISUAL RESULT, reported plainly: modest, well short of the anticipated headline. At the distant globe the whole disk shifts (max channel delta 101/255, mean 1.2) where the coarse cache under-resolved crater rims; at surface zoom the change is at most 1/255, because the refined cache's central difference already approximates the gradient there. The province-boundary shading seams SURVIVE, correctly: they are the bilinear interpolant's own gradient discontinuities at province cell centres (a field artifact that slice 9 retires), not a differencing artifact the analytic normal could fix. FLEXURE INTO THE SAMPLE: **STOPPED AT THE VALUE-AUTHORING LINE, NOT BUILT**, and the premise line is why. The task's premise (and `FLEXURE_ARC_SCOPE.md:13`, `CONSOLIDATED_SURFACE_PIPELINE.md:23`, and the kernel's own field doc `crates/physics/src/flexure.rs:312`) asserts T_e is "the DERIVED elastic lid thickness ... which the deep-time thermal state already carries". A code-state check plus an independent derivation-hunter agent PROVED IT DOES NOT: `ColumnState` is `{temperature, convecting}`, one LUMPED scalar per column, and NOTHING in `crates/` carries temperature on a DEPTH axis (no geotherm, no half-space cooling, no erf, no depth-resolved field), so a mechanical lid base cannot be located against a profile that does not exist. `PlateInputs` has no production caller; the kernel is still dormant. E and nu DO derive (the banked moduli route), and g and the densities are derived, so T_e is the SOLE unsupplied input to D. The tempting fixes are both authoring: `T_e = c * (thermal boundary layer)` invents c, and `T_e` = depth to a ~600 K limiting isotherm authors an empirical proxy that is not a floor constant and not dimensionless. The honest route (McNutt 1984 moment-equivalence, where the limiting isotherm EMERGES as a description rather than entering as a shortcut) needs three additions in dependency order: a depth-resolved geotherm T(z) across the lid (the bedrock gap), a pressure-dependent brittle branch (the built `derived_crust_yield_pa` is temperature- AND pressure-independent), and a SILICATE creep route (`crates/materials/src/creep.rs` is a complete Mukherjee-Bird-Dorn law in log-space and is dormant, but its diffusion input routes through `freezer::self_diffusivity` -> `MetallicRoute::cohesive_energy`, keyed by element symbol and scoped to ELEMENTAL METALS, so an olivine lid has no jump rate today). So the flexural middle is STILL EMPTY and the surface is still broad province swells plus tiny crater specks with nothing in between, which the zoom renders confirm. `SurfaceField`'s doc names the gap at the site: when T_e derives, flexure enters as one more analytic layer (deflection into `height_km`, the Green's function's analytic derivative into `gradient`) with no change to either function's shape. NEXT: the T_e substrate (a geotherm arc) before slice 5's render wiring can land. GEOTHERM ARC AUTHORIZED (2026-07-16, owner-ruled, `docs/working/GEOTHERM_ARC_SCOPE.md`): T_e is the SOLE unsupplied input to the flexural rigidity D, so the mid-scale relief band stays EMPTY until it derives (broad province swells plus tiny crater specks with nothing between, which is why the bumps do not read). THE DEFECT CHAIN HAS ONE AUTHOR, the ruling channel itself: the owner's coarseness ruling asserted 'the derived elastic lid thickness out of the thermal state', the coordinator's scope docs propagated that sentence, and `flexure.rs:312` carries it verbatim, but no derived elastic lid ever existed (`ColumnState` is {temperature, convecting}, one lumped scalar, nothing on a DEPTH axis). THE PREMISE LINE IS WIDENED (standing, effective now): any ruling premise of the form 'X is already DERIVED, CARRIED, or OWNED by the engine' is an IMPLEMENTATION-STATUS claim carrying the verify-or-condition line, identical to the wire verbs; the first rule caught only ACTION verbs and this claim's verb was 'derives from'. THE SKELETON (admit-the-alien checked): NO NEW STATE AXIS, T(z) is a DERIVED EVALUATOR rather than stored data. Surface temperature from insolation, the lumped scalar as the convecting interior's potential temperature, the lid profile between them the analytic conduction solution whose thickness comes from the flux the Ra machinery already computes (half-space erf where lids have ages, steady conductive for stagnant lids); thermal conductivity keys on MATERIAL CLASS before a Europa-class world renders (ice conductivity is strongly temperature-dependent where rock's is not, the convicting body). DEPENDENCY ORDER ratified: geotherm, then the BYERLEE brittle branch (pressure-dependent, an alien-admission gift because Byerlee is near material-INDEPENDENT for rock, one friction law for every silicate lid with ice the named deviant), then the SILICATE creep route (the Mukherjee-Bird-Dorn form STAYS; the activation energy routes through the engine's own 3b class constant, E* from g*R*T_m on the world's OWN melting temperature, so any material's creep derives from its own solidus, with measured olivine flow laws as calibrated anchor rows. EXPONENT RIDER checked: g is measured-class and T_m derived, so the product is class-grade in the exponent, the same legal status the freezer already relies on, band propagated). T_e then FALLS OUT of the YIELD-STRENGTH ENVELOPE (brittle curve meeting ductile curve at the world's own strain rate, itself derived from the convective timescale), and the ~600 K isotherm both shortcuts wanted to author is DEMOTED to what it always was: the Earth-olivine INSTANCE of the YSE construction, a hindcast cross-check (derived Earth T_e must reproduce oceanic T_e-versus-plate-age, with Mars and Venus elastic thickness as rows two and three). Nothing in the arc authors a scalar. THE IDENTICAL-CRUST ROOT (owner-sharpened): the flat-relief and identical-colour findings SHARE a root, ORBIT HAS NO EXPRESSION CHANNEL, because the channels through which orbit legitimately differentiates worlds at fixed seed (relief through the geotherm, surface state through climate, ice lines, and weathering) are respectively EMPTY and NOT YET BUILT. Part of the white-crust uniformity is therefore EXPECTED-MISSING rather than defect and retires on the already-sequenced hydrosphere arc; the DEFECT part is that colour does not consume the crust assemblage the engine already derives. #87 CORRECTED at the ruling: a single characteristic mass AS A DIVISOR stays FORBIDDEN; what #87 builds is the SFD NORMALIZATION INTEGRAL (per-bin mass from the reservoir's own material-class density, integrated over the distribution, normalized to the derived reservoir mass), and at Dohnanyi-class slopes the MASS integral is dominated by the LARGEST bodies, so the load-bearing piece is the TOP-END treatment (largest-remnant size from the assembly's own leftover statistics, or the fetched elbow as a tagged class instance), never anything at the small end. The two reservoirs STAY TWO (assembly debris behind the Leinhardt-Stewart wall vs the disk's un-accreted planetesimals: different origins, orbits, and flux histories, and late accretion draws on both with different time profiles), so the grep confusion is fixed IN THE GREP, never by merging the physics. SHORTCUT VALIDITY promoted to a STANDING RULE: a shortcut is valid exactly while its DEPARTURE from the parent form stays below the PARENT'S OWN BAND, derived per shortcut, never authored (the resolution rule applied to model-form error; the assembly's Eq.83-vs-Eq.82 crossover against the 0.43-dex scatter is its first instance). #45 CLOSED, stale by success: `Fixed::powf` and `cbrt` exist and are pinned under the Holsapple law. CONSUMED BANKED MACHINERY TWICE rather than rebuilding: the boundary layer L = d*Ra^(-1/3) was derived INLINE inside column_readout and is extracted to `laws::thermal_boundary_layer` (the geotherm is its SECOND consumer, and the driving stress and the geotherm must agree about lid thickness; sim geodynamics tests pass unchanged, so byte-identical), and `erfc` moved from private-in-ewald to `Fixed::erfc`/`erf` beside exp/ln/sqrt/cbrt/powf with ewald DELEGATING (the Madelung constants NaCl/CsCl/fluorite still pass, so behaviour-preserving). NUMERICAL TWIN in its NEW domain (the owner's condition: VALIDATION DOES NOT TRANSFER ACROSS DOMAINS; the A&S 7.1.26 fit was twinned over EWALD's argument range, the geotherm exercises eta = z/(2 sqrt(kappa t))), differenced against an INDEPENDENT composite-Simpson quadrature of erf's own definition sharing no code with the fitted series, agreeing to better than 1e-5 across eta = 0.25 to 3. HONEST LIMIT MEASURED: the A&S coefficients sum to 0.999999999, so erf(0) returns ~1.16e-9 rather than a clean zero, and the half-space surface boundary is honoured to ~1.16e-9*(T_i - T_s), microkelvin on a 1300 K contrast; the coordinator's docstring first claimed the boundary read 'exactly' and its OWN TEST convicted the claim. THE ISOTHERM IS DEAD (owner ruling, after the fetch read the primaries) AND NOTHING NUMERIC REPLACES IT. The arc's '~600 K' is a UNIT ERROR (327 C, BELOW every measured band; the classical statement is 450 +/- 150 C, in CELSIUS; Calmant et al. 1990: 'no estimate is close to the 600 C isotherm'), and it propagated as a ruling's summary statistic through the scope docs verbatim into geotherm.rs. THE DEEPER FINDING is why no corrected number replaces it: A LIMITING ISOTHERM IS NOT A PROPERTY OF THE LITHOSPHERE, it is a property of the lithosphere JOINED TO AN AGE CONVENTION (the SAME data give 550-600 C against thermal age and 350-450 C against isochron age, McNutt 1984 via Calmant; trenches diverge near 340 C), so it is a statistic with a HIDDEN CONDITIONING VARIABLE and could never have been a target: it would validate whichever convention it was silently born under. That is the SILENT-PARAMETER CLASS LIVING INSIDE THE LITERATURE, so DEFAULTS-TAKEN now extends to fetched rows' CONVENTIONS. The hindcast row is the MEASURED T_e-versus-age DATASET directly, with a MANDATORY AGE-CONVENTION FIELD per entry and the LOADING ENVIRONMENT SPLIT (oceanic interior loads primary, trenches a separate tagged environment); Mars (13 regions, Ruiz 2014) and Venus (trimodal, 47 percent below 20 km, Smrekar & Anderson 2005) are rows 2 and 3. Either way the low-stress regime ships with roughness + cohesion bands, and the conditioning axis is NORMAL STRESS through rho*g*z FIRST, material SECOND. Ice's frictional strength sits well below every rock, so ICE LIDS ARE WEAK ON BOTH BRANCHES. BYERLEE UNBLOCKED, and the dispute resolves IN THE AGENT'S FAVOUR: the USGS hosts the full 1978 paper openly, and the primary's own abstract settles the regime question (at low normal stress shear stress varies widely because friction is strongly dependent on SURFACE ROUGHNESS; at high normal stress that effect diminishes and friction becomes nearly independent of ROCK TYPE). So the universality floor IS effectively the 200 MPa branch point, the 0.85 branch below is a CENTRAL FIT THROUGH ROUGHNESS-SCATTERED DATA shipping with a WIDE BAND, and the three-regime recollection overstated the low-stress branch's tightness. THE KILOBAR INTERCEPT SETTLES BY ARITHMETIC THE ROW RUNS ON ITSELF: the branches are continuous at 200 MPa only if the intercept is 50 MPa (0.85 x 200 = 170 = 50 + 0.6 x 200), so that CONTINUITY IDENTITY ships as the row's SELF-TEST, and it convicts at least one widely read reference printing the intercept in megapascals. NAMED EXCEPTION BAND: montmorillonite/vermiculite gouge collapses friction far below both branches, so hydrated and altered fault materials are conditioned separately, which matters for exactly the water-processed crusts the hydrosphere arc will make. HOFMEISTER UNBLOCKED FROM THE ABSTRACT, and it CORRECTS THE RULING A SECOND TIME. The lattice term is kappa_298 * (298/T)^a * exp[-(4*gamma + 1/3) * integral(alpha d theta)] with a = 0.33 for SILICATES and 0.9 for MgO; the pressure dependence is d ln kappa / dP = (1/3 + 4 gamma)/K_T; the radiative term is the polynomial 0.0175 - 1.037e-4 T + 2.245e-7 T^2 - 3.407e-11 T^3 W/m/K when Fe2+ is present. THE INPUTS ARE ALL BANKED-COLUMN QUANTITIES (Gruneisen parameter, bulk modulus, thermal expansivity), so k lands as a DERIVED FORM on existing columns with per-mineral room-temperature anchors, BETTER than the anchor-constant row ordered. THE SELF-CORRECTION: '1/T for both classes' was STILL TOO COARSE; the honest shape is A POWER LAW WITH A CLASS-KEYED EXPONENT (near unity for simple lattices, ice measured at 612/T and MgO at 0.9, but 0.33 for complex silicates). SHAPE-FIRST WORKED AS DESIGNED: each fetch REFINED the exponent, none SUPPLIED the form. DISPUTE BAND (type-II, declared): modern high-pressure work finds radiative transport near 40 percent of olivine's conductivity at depth against Hofmeister's small pressure-independent polynomial, and the field calls the radiative role controversial; blast radius scoped honestly, since radiative transport GROWS WITH TEMPERATURE and the elastic lid is the COLD END of the column, so T_e is WEAKLY exposed and the band lands mostly on deep-mantle and slab-thermal consumers. HARTMANN SATURATION UNBLOCKED, and the fetch UPGRADES the ruling's own conditioning. The classical band is real and multiply attested (equilibrium at relative densities R of 0.1-0.3, five to ten percent of geometric saturation, the identified level fluctuating between ~0.4 and 2x itself; the equilibrium SFD of small craters runs as cumulative r^-2), which is the shape the render cap carries PER SIZE BIN rather than any scalar. BUT the modern observational result FORBIDS a universal coefficient: equilibrium density is NOT correlated with population age, can sit below one percent at some diameters, and depends on the production slope and the removal-rate distribution, while 57-160 km highland craters exceed R = 0.3 yet still follow the production function. So the cap ships as a BANDED CLASS OBJECT conditioned on the production SFD slope and the degradation regime. THE CONVICTING BODY IS THE MOON ALONE: size-dependent equilibrium on ONE surface, small maria craters saturated at a few percent while the large highland population never equilibrated. #87's saturation half unblocks on that row and composes cleanly with the count ruling: PRODUCTION-LIMITED BELOW the onset diameter, EQUILIBRIUM-SFD-CAPPED ABOVE it, both derived per surface age. THE ROW PROVES ITS OWN UNITS: Byerlee is published in KILOBARS, so reading tau = 0.5 + 0.6 sigma as MPa is a silent 100x error that has convicted a widely read reference, and the two branches are CONTINUOUS at the 200 MPa branch point ONLY if the intercept is 50 MPa (0.85 x 200 = 170 = 50 + 0.6 x 200). That identity is the module's SELF-TEST, and it holds BIT-EXACTLY: 0.85 and 0.6 each truncate slightly low in Q32.32 and land on the SAME product (730144440200 bits), so the branches meet with no residue between them, both sitting ~2.8e-8 MPa under the ideal 170. The test asserts the identity bit-exactly, the meeting VALUE at the representation's residue (my first draft demanded exactness and the test convicted me, the same trap the erf boundary taught), AND the guard's discriminating power explicitly: a kilobar-as-MPa intercept misses by ~49 MPa, ~49000x the tolerance. THE ALIEN INVERSION IS BUILT AND TESTED, not just documented: Byerlee's material-independence is a HIGH-STRESS property (above the 200 MPa branch point, per the primary's own abstract: at low normal stress shear stress varies widely because friction is strongly dependent on SURFACE ROUGHNESS; at high normal stress that diminishes and friction becomes nearly independent of ROCK TYPE), so the floor INVERTS the gift, since the worlds that never reach the universal regime are exactly the small low-gravity ones the rule meant to admit plus the shallowest km of everyone. `byerlee_is_in_the_universal_regime` makes that a QUESTION A CALLER ASKS rather than an assumption, and a standing test proves the inversion falls out of sigma_n = rho*g*z alone: 10 km into an Earth-gravity crust is past the branch point, 10 km into a lunar-gravity crust is still roughness-dominated. BRANCH-POINT REPAIR JUMPED THE QUEUE AND LANDED (owner ruling: THE BUILD ORDER IS A QUEUE FOR CONSTRUCTION, NOT FOR CORRECTION; repairs to landed defects JUMP IT whenever they are CHEAP AND BEHAVIOR-NEUTRAL where currently exercised). The defect was mine, one commit old: `byerlee_branch_point_mpa` hardcoded 200 MPa, which is the ROCK row wearing a constant's clothes, so `byerlee_is_in_the_universal_regime` would hand an ICE SHELL the rock boundary and quietly un-do the material conditioning the brittle branch had just gained, INSIDE THE VERY PREDICATE BUILT TO MAKE CONDITIONING EXPLICIT. CENSUS LINE RUN FIRST (the ruling's condition): NO production caller evaluates the predicate on any material class, so the repair is behavior-neutral by construction and both pins hold. THE AUDIT ADDITION CHANGED THE FIX'S SHAPE: ICE DOES NOT HAVE A BRANCH POINT, IT HAS A GAP. Rock's branch point is a CONTINUITY CROSSOVER (two laws meeting at 200 MPa, self-tested by the identity). Ice's two Beeman laws DO NOT MEET: the low law is licensed at or below 5 MPa, the high at or above 10, their naive mathematical crossing sits near 21 MPa OUTSIDE BOTH STATED DOMAINS, and at any splice inside the gap the fits disagree by several MPa, so a single spliced boundary would AUTHOR A DISCONTINUOUS STRENGTH LAW OUT OF THIN AIR. That is the n-gap finding wearing friction's coat. TREATMENT per that precedent: `FrictionLaw` carries `low_domain_max` and `high_domain_min` SEPARATELY (equal = crossover, unequal = gap), both laws ship VERBATIM on their STATED DOMAINS, and inside the gap `shear_strength_mpa` returns `ShearStrength::Bracket`, THE ENVELOPE THE TWO CITED FITS SPAN, containing ZERO chosen points, which is DERIVED information rather than an authored splice. Consumers eat bands natively; a verdict that flips across the bracket is near-degenerate and SURFACES. THE FLAGSHIP ALIEN-INVERSION TEST GAINS ITS MATERIAL CASE, completing a test that was valid but MATERIAL-BLIND (gravity covered, material now covered): a Europa-class shell at depth against Earth rock at depth, each past ITS OWN branch, plus the defect asserted so it cannot return (rock's row MISJUDGES the ice shell, calling it roughness-dominated where ice's own law has it on the high branch), plus the source's headline (ice yields below rock at the same stress: weak on BOTH branches). THE DAG QUESTION ANSWERED AND RULED: THE DAG ALREADY EXISTS AND WE ARE FLATTENING IT. `scripts/gen_floor_registry.py::scan_derives` reads hand-authored `// @derives[<id>]: <quantity> <- <inputs>` markers; the `<-` IS AN EDGE and the `[<id>]` is the generator's own declared MACHINE HANDLE, so the registry is a directed graph stored as a flat list and the tree is a RENDERING of data already present. AUTO-EXTRACTION PROHIBITED LOUDLY: a call graph masquerading as a derivation graph is this project's signature defect in another coat (a call edge is not a derivation edge; `ra_max` is a representable CAP, and an AST would happily make it a parent), so KEEP AUTHORSHIP HUMAN, MAKE THE CHECKING MECHANICAL (to the methods file as written). THREE GATE AMENDMENTS so it does not misfire: (1) THE DUAL GATE, the AST may NEVER AUTHOR an edge but MAY FALSIFY one, flagging a marker whose claimed inputs the computing function provably never reads, CONSERVATIVE FALSIFICATION ONLY, no completeness demanded (human authors the claim, machine referees it: shape-first wearing tooling clothes, and the answer to the registry's own stale line pointers); (2) THE DANGLING GATE KEYS ON PROVENANCE, only nodes claiming [D] owe in-edges, or every measured leaf and layer-4 draw fires on day one; (3) A DIAMOND IS NOT A DEFECT, AN UNARBITRATED DIAMOND IS: two providers with a REGISTERED LADDER ORDER and an OVERLAP SENTINEL are the conductivity ladder, LEGAL BY CONSTRUCTION, while two with neither are k/kappa, so the predicate is PROVIDERS-WITHOUT-REGISTERED-ARBITRATION or the gate convicts the best thing this arc built. RENDER-ON-DEMAND threads the needle: gate findings ship with their LOCAL SUBGRAPH drawn, the full tree browser stays second. THE SIXTH RULE, TERMS-DROPPED, answering the standing prophecy that the next break comes from where none of the five rules is looking: the SILENT PARAMETER HAS A SIBLING, THE SILENT OMISSION. Every governing equation in an arc doc carries a TERMS-DROPPED field listing what the form OMITS and the DOMAIN where the omission is valid (the erf profile drops distributed heating, valid where enrichment is negligible; rho*g*z drops pore pressure, valid where the fluid column is empty; a single-rate YSE drops load-timescale dependence, valid for one declared load class). DEFAULTS-TAKEN audits what the IMPLEMENTATION implied, CHORD-VARIABLES audits what the LITERATURE dropped, TERMS-DROPPED audits what the PHYSICS SPEC left out: together they cover WRITTEN, FETCHED, and UNWRITTEN. FIVE SPEC AMENDMENTS from the close audit, ALL pre-build so nothing landed reopens: (1) THE STRAIN RATE IS AN UNDECLARED CHORD VARIABLE INSIDE THE YSE SPEC ITSELF: T_e is not a property of a lithosphere, it is A CHORD OVER LOAD TIMESCALE (the same column supports a seamount over Myr, a rebounding ice load over kyr, and a tide over hours at THREE different elastic thicknesses, since ductile stress scales as strain rate^(1/n), ~2x per decade at n = 3.5), so the YSE evaluates at the strain rate OF THE LOAD BEING SUPPORTED, derived from the flexural curvature's own evolution rate, and the hindcast rows gain a SECOND conditioning field beside age convention: LOAD CLASS. THE CLOSURE, which is the whole case for the modality field in one sentence: THE LAUNDERED +/-0.5 HYPOTHETICAL WAS THE PRIMARY LITERATURE WARNING ABOUT EXACTLY THIS EXTRAPOLATION SENSITIVITY; the warning arrived as a number and its meaning was thrown away. (2) T(z) AS AUTHORIZED IS THE OCEANIC INSTANCE WIRED AS MECHANISM: the erf half-space carries no in-lid heat production, correct for oceanic lithosphere and wrong wherever the engine's own partition machinery works, since batch-melting enrichment concentrates heat producers into the crust (a large fraction of Earth's continental surface heat flow), steepening the shallow geotherm and THINNING T_e; convicting body ONE EARTH, TWO GEOTHERM FAMILIES, and reduced worlds whose uranium went coreward (Wohlers-Wood) take the OPPOSITE error from the same omission. Fix derive-first: distributed heating with H(z) read from the enrichment state, THE ERF PROFILE RECOVERED EXACTLY AS THE H -> 0 LIMIT, no fetched number. (3) THE BRITTLE BRANCH IS THE DRY LIMIT WIRED AS THE LAW: rho*g*z omits PORE-FLUID PRESSURE, first-order on any world with a fluid column (Earth's own fault-strength record; every ice shell over an ocean, where near-lithostatic pore pressure drives brittle strength toward ZERO). Fix: effective normal stress with the fluid-pressure ratio derived from the world's own hydrosphere and volatile state, DRY WORLDS REPRODUCING CURRENT BEHAVIOUR BIT-EXACTLY so the amendment is PIN-SAFE BY CONSTRUCTION, and the alien it admits is Europa. (4) the branch-point repair, landed above. THE DIAMOND GATE PULLED FORWARD AND RUN AS THE PRE-CREEP SWEEP (owner-ordered supervision upgrade, MECHANICAL not managerial: the two-site fixture was the THIRD instance of the two-providers shape in one week, found each time by a person running ONE LINE, and a person running one line is not a control). `scripts/diamond_gate.py`, a script over a registry that already existed. Findings ship with their LOCAL SUBGRAPH RENDERED, starting the render-on-demand path without waiting on the browser question. THE SWEEP FOUND THE KNOWN LIVE DEFECT MECHANICALLY (`thermal_diffusivity`, the k/kappa diamond), which was the point, plus TWO NAME-COLLISION defects nobody knew about: `friction` (the FIELDS are the material's Coulomb COEFFICIENT mu, read from `mech.kinetic_friction`; the LAW computes a friction FORCE: different quantities, one name) and `weight` (`laws::weight` is physical weight mg; the seven fields are neural weights, priorities, and tallies). Both discharge by route 3, RENAME. Plus one false-positive class, OUTPUT CACHES (`convective_stress`: the field STORES the law's result and its doc says so). THE GATE IS NOT --strict-READY and ships as a REPORTING SWEEP, stated plainly rather than shipped as a gate that cries wolf. THE REFINEMENT THAT WAS TRIED AND REVERTED, AND THE RULE IT EARNED, both recorded IN the script because the next person will propose it again: the output-cache class looked mechanically fixable (exempt any field whose doc cites the law computing it, which `convective_stress` does). THAT REFINEMENT SILENCED THE ONE TRUE POSITIVE. `ColumnParams.thermal_diffusivity` ALSO cites `laws::thermal_diffusivity`, because its doc is the k/kappa TAG explaining that the field CONFLICTS with that law by 20x. A CACHE CITES ITS LAW; A DOCUMENTED CONFLICT CITES ITS LAW TOO; the citation does not distinguish them. So the exemption made the gate BLIND to the exact defect it exists to find, and it did so QUIETLY: the sweep just got shorter and cleaner-looking. THE RULE: A REFINEMENT THAT MAKES A GATE QUIETER MUST BE PROVEN NOT TO MAKE IT BLIND, against the gate's own known true positives, BEFORE IT SHIPS. A gate's noise is visible and annoying; a gate's blindness is invisible and comfortable, which is why blindness is the failure mode that survives review. FIVE STRUCTURAL CONDITIONS ON THE CREEP SLICE (owner, since creep is the most rider-sensitive machinery in the engine): (1) THE EXPONENT GATE RUNS AT INGESTION, since E* + P*V* over RT lives in an Arrhenius exponential, so every quantity entering it is GRADE-CHECKED AS A TEST (measured E*, interval-tagged V* consumed by pressure regime, derived T_m for the g-route estimator) and NOTHING ESTIMATOR-GRADE CROSSES INTO THE EXPONENT without the rider's escalation; (2) THE WATER VARIABLE GETS THE KILOBAR DEFENSE: the wet rows are FUGACITY-referenced and the fetch's own hazard section named feeding H per 10^6 Si into them as the exact silent error, so water content ships as a NEWTYPE ENCODING ITS REFERENCE FRAME and the wrong reference FAILS TO TYPECHECK rather than fails to be noticed; (3) THE ROW SCHEMA KEYS ON MECHANISM AND WATER STATE JOINTLY, so a Dixon-style composite across two rows PHYSICALLY CANNOT BE ASSEMBLED from the table; (4) THE STRAIN-RATE AMENDMENT IS A DAY-ONE INPUT, the YSE intersecting at the load's own rate with the convention declared, never retrofitted after T_e exists; (5) THE A-SOURCE RETIREMENT CHECKLIST CARRIES BOTH SITES, since the fixture cluster provably lives at two call sites that can drift independently and killing one while the other feeds heat production would be THE REPAIR THAT ISN'T. STANDING PRACTICE ADOPTED: EVERY REPAIRED DEFECT SHIPS WITH ITS OWN WRONGNESS ASSERTED (the branch-point repair's test asserts that rock's row MISJUDGES the ice shell, encoding the defect as a must-hold fact rather than a fixed bug), WHICH IS WHAT MAKES A REPAIR PERMANENT INSTEAD OF RECENT. And the honest accounting, said out loud by the channel that owns it: the prediction was that the next break would come from where none of the five rules was looking, and it did, INTO A SPEC RATHER THAN A BUILD, TWICE OVER; the sixth rule now looks there, the agents already look there by habit, and THE RESIDUAL RISK SURFACE OF THIS PROJECT IS, ON THE CURRENT RECORD, THE DOCUMENTS THIS CHANNEL WRITES. CREEP'S MEASURED RUNG LANDED (`crates/physics/src/creep_rows.rs`, DORMANT, both pins hold), and the PREMISE CHECK CHANGED ITS SHAPE BEFORE A LINE WAS WRITTEN: `civsim_materials::creep` (Mukherjee-Bird-Dorn) and H&K's Table 1 are DIFFERENT PARAMETERIZATIONS WHOSE PREFACTORS ARE NOT INTERCHANGEABLE. MBD is `eps_dot = A (sigma/G)^n (b/d)^p [D G b/(kT)]` with A DIMENSIONLESS, stress normalized by the shear modulus, grain size by the Burgers vector, and the Arrhenius inside D (the freezer's jump rate); H&K is `eps_dot = A sigma^n d^-p f_H2O^r exp(-(E*+PV*)/RT)` with A in the TABLE'S OWN UNITS, raw stress, an explicit Arrhenius, and A WATER-FUGACITY TERM MBD DOES NOT HAVE AT ALL. Feeding H&K's A = 1.1e5 into the MBD prefactor would be a SILENT UNIT CATASTROPHE. So CREEP IS A LADDER (MBD = derived estimator rung via the freezer's E* = g*R*T_m route; H&K = measured anchor rung, which is what the ruling's 'measured olivine flow laws as the CALIBRATED ANCHOR ROWS' already said), REGISTERED in the diamond gate so the two providers are arbitrated rather than colliding. THE FIVE CONDITIONS, each realized: (1) THE EXPONENT GATE AT INGESTION (`Modality` + `exponent_admits`): only Measured/Fitted cross into `exp(-(E*+PV*)/RT)`, since a grade error there MULTIPLIES through an exponential rather than adding; H&K's two GBS rows FAIL IT BY CONSTRUCTION because their energies are ASSUMED, transferred from easy-slip data (footnote f), never fitted to GBS. (2) THE WATER FRAME IS A TYPE (`WaterContent::Fugacity{mpa}` vs `Hydroxyl{h_per_10e6_si}`): the wet rows are FUGACITY-referenced, the prior fetch INVERTED exactly this, and feeding H/10^6Si to a fugacity row now FAILS TO TYPECHECK rather than failing to be noticed. (3) THE ROW IS ATOMIC, identity `(mechanism, water_state)` JOINTLY, so the DIXON COMPOSITE CANNOT BE ASSEMBLED: E* = 400 appears exactly once (dry GBS below 1250 C), that row is DRY with r = '-', and his r = 1.2 comes from a row two axes away (different mechanism AND different water state). (4) THE STRAIN RATE IS A DAY-ONE INPUT, never retrofitted. (5) The A-source checklist carries BOTH sites, tracked on the board. V* SHIPS AS INTERVAL-TAGGED DETERMINATIONS consumed BY PRESSURE REGIME (`ActivationVolume::covers`, `select_activation_volume`): the lid reads low-pressure chords, the deep interior high-pressure ones, and a consumer outside every interval gets NONE rather than the nearest number, because reaching for it would be extrapolating a chord past its endpoints. AND THE MODULE'S OWN TEST CAUGHT A 10x ERROR IN A CREEP PREFACTOR, mine, written minutes earlier: `ln(1.1e5)` was hand-written as `ln(1.1) + 4*ln(10)` (9.31) where 1.1e5 needs FIVE decades (11.61), and `6500 = 6.5e3` carried the same off-by-one. A prefactor multiplies the rate DIRECTLY, so both were factor-of-ten errors arriving as plausible numbers with no symptom. Repaired with `ln_scientific(mantissa, den, power_of_ten)`, which makes the exponent something the caller STATES rather than something the caller COUNTS IN THEIR HEAD, and all three prefactors are now pinned by the test that caught them.

Four derived pieces. THE TRIGGER (`schonberg_chandrasekhar_limit`): `q_max = 0.37*(mu_env/mu_core)^2`, ~0.074 for a helium core under a hydrogen envelope, the star leaves the main sequence when the growing core fraction crosses it (Schonberg-Chandrasekhar 1942). THE TEMPERATURE ATTRACTOR (`hayashi_effective_temperature`): the Hayashi boundary pins the photosphere into the cited ~2000-4000 K band almost independent of luminosity, the engine's own H-minus opacity steepness the physical basis (the envelope forgets its history). THE LUMINOSITY (`shell_burning_luminosity`): the calibrated shell-burning homology `L = 238000*mu^3*Z_CNO^0.04*(M_c^2 - 0.0305*M_c - 0.1802)` L_sun (Kippenhahn/Refsdal-Weigert), ~1e4 L_sun at M_c=0.66 solar, with TWO LOUD DOMAIN FLAGS (below 0.5 solar L is not a function of core mass alone; above 0.8 solar the envelope convection penetrates the burning shell and the linear relation fails, the radiation-pressure regime where L is proportional to core mass alone). THE CLOCK (`core_growth_rate_msun_per_myr`): `dM_c/dt = L/(X_env*E_H)`, ~0.14 M_sun/Myr, with E_H derived from the cited hydrogen mass-defect fraction (0.00712) times the fundamental c^2 (~6.4e14 J/kg). Sun-relative fixed-point (L in L_sun, R in R_sun via `stellar_radius_rsun`) keeps the supergiant representable, the astro.rs discipline. DEMONSTRATION (test `a_betelgeuse_mass_star_is_a_red_supergiant_by_construction`): an 18 M_sun post-MS star derives T_eff=3500 K (RED) and R=964 R_sun (huge, Betelgeuse ~764 R_sun scale) from a core-set L~1.26e5 L_sun forced through the Hayashi pin. - IN PROGRESS (orbital-mechanics arc #78, the "orbits arc", branch claude/seam4-deeptime): SLICE 1 LANDED (dormant, byte-neutral, both pins hold): the KEPLER PERIOD now DERIVES. `astro::kepler_orbital_period_seconds(orbit_au, star_mass_ratio)` = T_ref*sqrt(orbit_au^3/star_mass_ratio) from Kepler's third law T^2 = 4*pi^2*a^3/(G*M_star), with `reference_orbital_period_seconds()` the derived 1-AU-1-M_sun anchor (2*pi*sqrt(AU^3/(G*M_sun)) from the cited AU, solar mass, and fundamental G, rooted once by the scale-aware Tier-2 isqrt). It derives the sidereal-grade year (~3.155e7 s, ~365.25 days), distinct from and retiring the celestial substrate's round 365.0-day fixture (`OrbitalElements::dev_earth` = 31,536,000 s, whose own doc names Kepler's third law its north star). 4 tests: Earth's year within 0.01% of the Julian year, the a^1.5 / M^-0.5 scaling, an INDEPENDENT Jupiter check (11.86 yr reproduced from orbit + solar mass, no fit), fail-loud on bad inputs and far orbits. HONEST UNITS LIMIT surfaced (and it is load-bearing for the multi-body arc): the period IN SECONDS crosses the Q32.32 ceiling at ~16 AU around a solar-mass star, so a Kuiper (~40 AU) or Oort (~1e4-1e5 AU) body's year-in-seconds is NOT representable in one Fixed. Deriving the period in YEARS (or reference-period units) instead of seconds keeps it representable to ~1e6 AU (well past Oort); this units choice, and the deep-time-vs-orbital-phase clock split, is the multi-body timestepping question the owner raised. Wiring the derivation onto the run path (retiring `dev_earth`) moves the year value 365.0 -> 365.25 days, so it re-baselines the pins and is a held run-path slice. NEXT slices: orbit position (analytic Kepler-equation phase), spin + axial tilt, sun-direction lighting (retire the viewer's authored screen-space star_dir), the projecting camera. SLICE 2 LANDED (dormant, byte-neutral, default pin holds): the ANALYTIC ORBITAL PHASE, a new module `sim/src/orbit.rs`. `orbital_state(mean_anomaly, eccentricity)` solves Kepler's equation M = E - e*sin(E) for the eccentric anomaly by Newton's method (fixed 20-step count, deterministic, from the E0 = M + e*sin(M) guess, using the CORDIC Fixed sin/cos) and reads off the perifocal position (x/a = cos E - e, y/a = sqrt(1-e^2) sin E, focus at the star), the star distance r/a = 1 - e*cos E, and the true anomaly (a from-scratch atan2 built on Fixed::atan with quadrant correction). ANALYTIC not stepped: the position is exact at any time from (phase, eccentricity) with no accumulated dt, exactly the fast-orbital-phase half of the deep-time clock split; the mean anomaly is unit-free (2*pi * fraction of period), so it is independent of the seconds-vs-years period-unit question. 5 tests: circular orbit E=nu=M and r/a=1, perihelion/aphelion distances 1-e and 1+e, the Kepler residual E - e*sin E = M at e=0.45, the geometric invariant x^2+y^2 = (r/a)^2 at e=0.6, determinism + fail-loud on unbound orbits (e >= 1, e < 0). NEXT: sun-direction lighting (the orbital position + spin/axial tilt gives the sub-solar point, retiring the viewer's authored star_dir), then the projecting camera. SLICE 3 LANDED (dormant, byte-neutral, default pin holds, in `sim/src/orbit.rs`): the SUN-DIRECTION GEOMETRY. `star_unit_orbital_plane(&state)` gives the planet-to-star unit vector in the orbital plane (the raw sun direction the lighting reads), and `solar_declination(&state, obliquity, perihelion_longitude)` derives the SUB-SOLAR LATITUDE (the seasons): sin(decl) = sin(obliquity)*sin(true_anomaly + perihelion_longitude), which swings between +/- the obliquity over one orbit (the tropics), zero at the equinoxes, and carries the eccentric orbit's uneven season lengths for free because the season angle uses the TRUE anomaly. obliquity and perihelion_longitude are per-world arguments (admit-the-alien). Also HARDENED `atan2` (used by the true-anomaly read): it now divides the smaller magnitude by the larger, so the near-vertical case (cos near zero at the top/bottom of every orbit, where a naive y/x overflowed fixed point and returned None) is exact; this was a latent bug the seasons test surfaced. 7 orbit tests total (added: star direction is unit and points at the focus, the seasons trace equinox=0 / solstice=+/-tilt / untilted=no-seasons). NEXT: the full body-frame sun direction with spin (sub-solar longitude / time of day), then the viewer wiring that retires the authored star_dir + the projecting camera. SLICE 4 LANDED (dormant, byte-neutral, default pin holds): the ILLUMINATION MATH that completes the derivation the lighting reads. `subsolar_longitude(spin_phase)` derives the meridian under the star from the rotation phase (the sun sweeps west as the body spins east, folded to [-pi, pi], the time-of-day clock). `solar_elevation_cosine(lat, lon, declination, subsolar_longitude)` = sin(lat)sin(decl) + cos(lat)cos(decl)cos(lon - subsolar_lon), the cosine of the star's zenith angle (the Lambert illumination): +1 with the star overhead at the sub-solar point, 0 on the terminator, negative on the night side. So from the DERIVED sun position (declination from orbit + tilt, sub-solar longitude from spin) a renderer lights any tile at (lat,lon) by the positive part, replacing any authored light direction. 10 orbit tests (added: the sub-solar longitude sweeps west with spin; the elevation is overhead at the sub-solar point and underfoot at the antipode; the equinox-equator day/night cycle noon=1/dusk=0/midnight=-1, pole-on-terminator=0). NEXT: the VIEWER WIRING (feed orbit->declination->elevation into render.rs, retire the authored screen-space star_dir), then the projecting camera. VIEWER FEATURE LANDED (2026-07-15, delegated build, manager-gated, default pin holds, viewer-only so non-canon): (a) DERIVED LIGHTING retires the authored star_dir: `render::sub_solar_body_dir(declination, subsolar_longitude)` feeds draw_globe's Lambert term the body-frame sub-solar vector, so the shading reads out the physical solar_elevation_cosine (a test proves N.S == orbit::solar_elevation_cosine); obliquity and eccentricity are READ per-world from `DiurnalSky` (`sky.obliquity` 0.4091 rad, `sky.eccentricity`, whose values live in sim as Earth's cited data), NOT authored in the viewer (owner correction actioned: zero attitude literals in the viewer; axis orientation/phase/rotation are reserved per-world SceneAttitude fields labeled R-CELESTIAL-SECULAR #44). The day/night terminator and the seasons animate as observability playback sweeps (frame counts, not physical rotation values). (b) SYSTEM-MAP DEFAULT VIEW: `render::render_system_map` draws the star (blackbody colour) at centre, each planet's orbit ellipse from `orbit::orbital_state`, and a dot per planet; run_derived samples 5 orbits (0.7-1.5 AU), each independently derived, HUD+comment stating these are sampled independently-derived worlds NOT an emergent system (#72). (c) CLICK-WOOSH: left-click a dot smoothstep-eases a 38-frame zoom down to that planet's derived-lit globe, Escape woosh back. (d) headless `--system-map <path>` mode. Verified: --system-map renders 900x700 non-blank (4 planets, 308 colours), --derived-globe's lit hemisphere tracks the derived sun, default pin 40fe8a72... unchanged, 29 viewer tests pass, fmt+clippy clean. Frame remap noted: the sub-solar vector is (cos*decl*sin*sslon, sin*decl, cos*decl*cos*sslon) in draw_globe's y-up/z-prime-meridian frame (proven by the N.S identity test). UNITS FIX LANDED (2026-07-15, dormant, byte-neutral, default pin holds): the period-in-YEARS derivation that retires the ~16 AU seconds ceiling for the multi-body map. `astro::kepler_orbital_period_years(orbit_au, star_mass_ratio)` = sqrt(orbit_au^3/star_mass_ratio) in astronomical units (AU, solar mass, sidereal year), computed in LOG-SPACE (ln T = (3 ln orbit_au - ln mass_ratio)/2, the planet_radius_m cube-root precedent) so orbit_au^3 never forms; representable past the Oort cloud (~1e6 yr at 1e5 AU) where the seconds form overflowed at ~16 AU. Fail-loud past the representable-years ceiling (~1.6e6 AU), the guard being ln(2^31) = 31*ln(2), the log of the Q32.32 maximum itself (an engine bound derived from the representation, not an owner value). 2 tests: Earth=1yr / Jupiter=11.86 / Neptune=165 (past the seconds ceiling, which is shown to overflow there) / Oort-1e4-AU=~1e6yr; and years*sidereal == seconds (one physics two units), the a^1.5 scaling, fail-loud past the ceiling. This is the grounding agent's finding that NO new representation type is needed (Q32.32 spans ~19 decades; the whole range is ~11, so seconds failed on CENTERING not span). The run-path manifest field rename (orbital_period_seconds -> years) + the state-hash fold (fold the derived u64 cadence to hold the pins) is the HELD run-path integration for the owner's fold call.
- IN PROGRESS (small-body buildout #74, the "asteroids and comets" arc, branch claude/seam4-deeptime): SLICE 1 LANDED (dormant, byte-neutral, both pins hold): the UN-ACCRETED PLANETESIMAL RESIDUE now instantiates as DISCRETE small bodies whose orbit and composition DERIVE, in a new module `sim/src/smallbody.rs` (`DiskReservoir`, `SmallBody`, `derive_small_body`). COMPOSITION (asteroid vs comet) is the water snow line: a body is refractory inside and icy beyond, split where the disk temperature (`astro::disk_effective_temperature`, the two-regime irradiation+viscous profile) crosses the water condensation temperature, decided by evaluating the Murphy-Koop ice saturation curve (`physics::ice_sublimation`, the cited [M] equation coefficients read via `equation_coefficients()`) at that temperature against the nebular water partial pressure. Derive-not-fit: for the Sun-and-solar-nebula fixture the snow line lands ~2.4 AU (near the real ~2.7 AU belt edge) with no fit to that orbit. ORBIT (semi-major axis) is the inverse of the residual disk-mass distribution (`astro::disk_surface_density` integrated `2*pi*r*Sigma(r)`, the planet's feeding zone masked so no body lands in the swept gap). SIZE is the inverse of the Dohnanyi SFD (`world::impact_flux::number_fraction_above_size`), the SAME distribution the seam-4 impact/crater chain draws strikes from, so the meteoroids are its small tail, not re-derived. ECCENTRICITY is the Rayleigh viscous-stirring inverse (shape derived, scale reserved). 11 tests (snow-line split, snow-line orbit in the few-AU band, ice-condensation follows the saturation curve, Murphy-Koop numerical twin, the size sampler round-trips impact_flux, the swarm is small-dominated, orbits span the disk and avoid the swept gap, the Rayleigh median, an end-to-end rocky-near/icy-far body, an alien reservoir is a data row, fail-soft). RESERVED-WITH-BASIS (surfaced, not fabricated): the nebular water partial pressure (solar water mole fraction x local disk pressure; the ~150-182 K Lodders snow line it implies is robust to ~10 K against a factor-100 pressure change because the saturation curve is exponentially steep) and the eccentricity stirring scale (viscous-stirring RMS e, ~0.1 main-belt-grade); the disk inner/outer edge (inner truncation, outer set by the surface-density cutoff r_c); the rest are inherited astro/impact_flux residues. Stone 0 clean (one classified deser row for the cited Murphy-Koop coefficients).
