- TOWARD #72 (accretion primitives, dormant, byte-neutral, default pin holds, `sim/src/astro.rs`): two rungs of the emergent-system ruler. HILL RADIUS `hill_radius_au(orbit_au, planet_mass_earth, star_mass_ratio)` = a*(M/(3*M_star))^(1/3), the reach of a body's gravity against the star's tide (the Earth-to-Sun mass ratio folds once from the two cited anchors, so the cube root runs on an order-1e-6 value); two independent anchors matched with no fit (Earth ~0.0098 AU, Jupiter ~0.355 AU). ISOLATION MASS `isolation_mass_earth(orbit_au, star_mass_ratio, sigma, C)` = the Kokubo-Ida oligarchic closed form (2*pi*C*a^2*Sigma)^(3/2)/sqrt(3*M_star), which RETIRES the reserved feeding-zone width (it now derives as C Hill radii); the honest result is SUB-EARTH at 1 AU (a Mars-class oligarch, which is why Earth needs mergers to reach one mass). Run in LOG-SPACE, which needed a general fix to `physics::saha::ln_of_decimal` to normalize a WIDE plain integer (the AU in metres overflowed Q32.32 before the log); the fix carries its own test and a deserialization baseline classification (the Stone 0 gate correctly blocked the new from_decimal_str sites and I classified them rather than overriding). NEXT: tile the disk with planets spaced by mutual Hill radii, consuming these two, so a multi-body system emerges (#72).
- GPU i128/trig FINDING (2026-07-15, delegated + gated, crates/gpu only, pins unaffected): the owner is RIGHT that CUDA does i128 and trig is fully featured; the earlier "no i128" was a CubeCL DSL limit, not a CUDA one. PROVEN: the direct `((a as i128)*(b as i128))>>32` does NOT compile in a `#[cube]` kernel (`i128: CubePrimitive is not satisfied`); cubecl-ir's `IntKind` is only {I8,I16,I32,I64} on the released crate AND on `main` (an upgrade would not add it). But the exact `__int128` device kernel compiles through NVRTC with `--device-int128` to real 128-bit PTX (confirmed on the 5090, CUDA 12.9), so the target can do it, CubeCL just does not surface it. Wiring i128 through CubeCL is a large cross-crate fork (add I128 to IntKind + the frontend traits + each backend; SPIR-V has no native 128-bit) for ZERO correctness gain: the u16-limb `q32_mul` already reproduces `Fixed::mul` bit-for-bit and is backend-general, so the limb primitives are load-bearing, not a workaround to retire. TRIG confirmed: sin/cos/atan/asin + exp/ln/powf/sqrt all pass bit-identity gates on the 5090 (a CubeCL CPU-backend constant-prop overflow bug means trig bit-identity is provable on CUDA only; Stage-0 arithmetic is bit-identical on both). LANDED: `crates/gpu/tests/cpu_backend_gate.rs`, a device-free Stage-0 bit-identity gate on the CubeCL CPU backend (runs with no GPU), plus a doc note at the multiply's home. 12 CUDA gates pass on the 5090; the GPU crate is excluded from default-members so the run pins are untouched. DISPATCHER BUILT (2026-07-15, two parallel agents, both crates/gpu only, pins unaffected): a runtime i128-capability detector (NVRTC-compile `__int128` with `--device-int128`, cached, catch_unwind fallback) + the `gpu_mul_i128` kernel + a `gpu_mul_auto`/`gpu_mul_best` dispatcher + `tests/mul_i128_gate.rs` proving the `__int128` kernel bit-identical to `Fixed::mul` AND to the CubeCL limb multiply over corners + a 1M/1M-element sweep on the 5090 (PASS). The two agents diverged only on the PERF interpretation, and the divergence reconciles: both agree there is NO 128-bit hardware ALU (NVRTC synthesizes `__int128` from 32-bit ops) and the kernel is CUDA-only, so it stays a proven-equal OPT-IN dispatch, never the canonical backend-general multiply (the u16-limb `q32_mul` stays canonical + portable). The 6x-vs-1.63x gap is two different comparison points, both real: agent 617294f compared the i128 kernel to the limb WRAPPER (host-side i64->u32-half split, ~179ms) and correctly diagnosed most of the 6x as HOST-wrapper overhead, FIXABLE WITHOUT i128; agent 063c22c compared the two KERNELS device-to-device (pre-split, CUDA-event timed) and measured a real on-device 1.63x (native 51.4 vs limb 31.5 Gops/s), backed by PTX instruction counts 26 vs 211 (NVRTC's u32-wide 64x64->128 lowering vs the hand-written u16 sign-magnitude schoolbook), memory-bound-capped for a bare multiply and paying off only when FUSED in a compute-bound kernel. Net actionable levers: (1) fix the limb wrapper's host split (portable, no i128), (2) the u16 kernel could go u32-limb to close most of the 1.63x portably, (3) the `__int128` kernel is the opt-in CUDA path. Integration of the cleaner build (063c22c) pending; neither merged yet.

- PARTIAL: a being picks a plant for its PARTS (not just grazes it) is unproven; the grazing path is done, the pick-for-resources seam is the biosphere-meets-made-world integration. FOUNDATION building: corrected-T3 (Agent C) makes whole-plant food value DERIVE from the plant's own material composition (its substances' `bio.energy_density` floor axis), so a woody plant is less nutritious than a fruity one and an alien plant is a data row. The PER-PART follow-on (owner-ratified 2026-07-09) is the same derivation per part: a plant's parts (bark edible, woody core not, fruiting bodies as distinct organs) carry different compositions and a being chooses which part to eat. FULLER VISION (owner-articulated 2026-07-09, "a plant is a growing, depleting, multi-part matter body"): the derive-first spine is that a plant is a BODY of matter with parts, the same substrate a creature body uses (promoted parts, tissues-as-composition, located matter), so almost none of it is new mechanism. Already built and reusable: WHICH creature can eat WHICH part is the consumer's own metabolism (`physical_intake` keys on the eater's assimilation, so a cellulose-digester banks the woody stem and a fruit-eater does not, no plant-side edibility tag); the whole-plant value derives from composition (corrected-T3); and eating REMOVES matter (grazing depletes the cell producer supply, mass-conserving, and the matter cycle regrows it), though today at the cell not bite-by-bite from a part. The ONE piece that is new is the plant as a GROWING, DEPLETING INDIVIDUAL: it accumulates matter and its composition shifts as it ages (a sapling is not a mature tree), a bite drops its remaining value, picking a fruit removes that part; this turns a plant from a field supply into an individual body with a growth-and-depletion trajectory, and couples to the MULTI-CELL spatial-extent item below (a big plant spanning cells). Scope-as-one-arc when the owner wants it built.

This is the substrate the per-part food above and larger-bodied creatures both need: a multi-cell plant's parts sit in different cells, a creature bigger than a cell occupies a region. The COMPLETE byte-neutrality reason (the section-9 confirmation-bias lens caught that my first two justifications each named a secondary cause and missed the primary; verified against source): the delivery path is off all four pins by construction (strike opt-in); on the grade path, PRIMARILY, no pinned affordance registry (`dev_default` for default/discovery, `dev_geophage` for viability/full, run_world.rs:255/264/268) arms an IMPACT-gated affordance (POUND `requires ID_IMPACT` lives only in `dev_striker`, never installed by run_world), so `tool_capability(..., ID_IMPACT)` is never invoked and the IMPACT grade (with its new elastic term) never runs on any pinned scenario. Defense in depth: even if it were armed, `tool_capability`'s `geo` exposes `mech.contact_area`/`mech.mass` but never the `mech.cross_section_area`/`mech.stroke_length` the IMPACT kernel reads, so IMPACT-via-tool is pre-existingly zero (both rigid and elastic) regardless of the tool substance's `mat.elastic_modulus` (iron carries it); the grown-segment path (`morphogen::segment_capabilities`) supplies that geometry but grows no `mat.elastic_modulus` and its `grow()` runs on no pinned scenario; the catalog-part path scores only PIERCE/LOCOMOTE/REFRACT, never IMPACT. The grade/delivery LOCKSTEP the gate ruled (iv) holds at the SEGMENT level (a being's own actuator: `segment_capabilities` and `strike_*`'s `resolve_delivered_energy` read the same segment axes and the same MAX); the `tool_capability(ID_IMPACT)` path is pre-existingly zero (a separate step-1 seam, a tool exposes mass not cross_section/stroke), flagged not fixed here. SLICE 4 BUILT (the hydraulic kernel, byte-neutral, the last mechanical-family member; `26d7979`): the gate's slice-4 directive was build the `integral P dV` law OR prove `actuator_work` composes, and it COMPOSES with NO new law: for an incompressible fluid at constant driving pressure `integral P dV = P (A d) = (P A) d = F d`, so `TransferKernel::Hydraulic` is `actuator_work(stress_force(fluid.driving_pressure, cross_section), stroke)`, the SAME two floor laws the rigid kernel uses keyed on the fluid driving pressure (megapascal-stored, so the same MPa-to-N bridge applies), a hydrostat actuator (an octopus arm, a spider's hydraulic leg, a water jet) a data row not a new law; `resolve_delivered_energy` is now the MAX over {rigid, elastic, hydraulic} (exhaustive match `Kinetic | ElasticRecoil | Hydraulic`), the row gains a `pressure_axis`, and the IMPACT grade reads the same three-way MAX (the lockstep test pins the fourth axis). The COMPRESSIBLE gas-expansion case (P falls over the stroke, the true varying-P integral reading `fluid.bulk_modulus` + an equation of state) does NOT reduce to `F d` and is the flagged future kernel that would need a new law; reusing the piston cross-section as the fluid channel area is a proxy, the dedicated `fluid.channel_radius`-derived area flagged as the reserved refinement. FRONT-END SLICE 2 (disk thermal structure, the next rung) landed byte-neutral: `civsim_sim::astro::irradiated_disk_temperature` derives the disk mid-plane temperature `T(r)` at an orbit from irradiation balance, reusing `stellar_flux` for the flux `F(r)` the annulus intercepts and `radiative_equilibrium` for the fourth root (`sigma*T^4 = reprocessing_factor*F(r)`), so `T` falls as `r^(-1/2)` (the slope that places the condensation snow lines the next rung reads). DERIVE-NOT-FIT anchor proven: at 1 AU with the isotropic-reradiator factor (1/4) it derives ~278.2 K, Earth's textbook blackbody equilibrium temperature (the ~255 K real value is this reduced by the ~0.3 albedo the atmosphere arc supplies later), from `L_sun`, the AU, and the derived `sigma` alone. The Mie kernel LANDED byte-neutral: `civsim_physics::opacity::mie_q_abs(x, n, k)` derives the absorption efficiency `Q_abs = Q_ext - Q_sca` of a homogeneous sphere from the BHMIE recurrence (Bohren-Huffman 1983 App. A: downward `D_n(mx)` from `nmx = max(nstop,|mx|)+15`, upward Riccati-Bessel `psi_n`/`chi_n`, Wiscombe `nstop = x + 4x^(1/3) + 2`, coefficients `a_n`/`b_n`, `Q_ext = (2/x^2) sum (2n+1) Re(a_n+b_n)`, `Q_sca` the squared-magnitude sum), keyed on per-particle `(n,k)` DATA (admit-the-alien: a metal or exotic condensate is a different row). Runs in DETERMINISTIC wide-fixed complex arithmetic (a plain-i128 value at scale 2^64, BigRat borrowed ONLY as the wide intermediate for a product or quotient since `chi_n^2 ~ 2e10` overflows Q32.32's norm_sq and i128 cannot hold the `a*b` product), FAIL-LOUD on any overflow (returns None), valid over `[0.1, 50]` (below: the exact Rayleigh form; above: the geometric limit `Q_ext -> 2`). Verified against the BHMIE f64 reference AND a Python wide-fixed reference (matches to 9 digits): `Q_abs(1, 1.5+0.01i)=0.02884`, `Q_abs(3, 1.5+0.1i)=0.89525`, `Q_abs(6, 1.68+0.03i)=0.80626`, plus the Rayleigh linear-in-x reduction (the guard against the classic BHMIE off-by-one that scales as 1/x). 6 Mie tests, 313 physics total, pins hold. Five prove-before-trust catches shaped the numerics: unreduced-BigRat geometric blowup (the complex reciprocal squares the denominator), reduced-BigRat 48k-bit growth on generic Q32.32 inputs, the Q32.32 norm_sq overflow, the i128 `a*b` overflow that Python bigints masked, and the SCALE=64 / `[0.1, 50]` overflow-floor. The SIZE-DISTRIBUTION INTEGRAL LANDED byte-neutral: `civsim_physics::opacity::grain_size_averaged_opacity(lambda, n, k, rho, slope, a_min, a_max)` derives the size-averaged grain mass absorption coefficient `kappa_abs(lambda) = (3/(4 rho)) <a^2 Q_abs>/<a^3>` over a power-law distribution `n(a) ~ a^-slope`, with `grain_qabs(x, n, k)` dispatching the single-sphere `Q_abs` across the three regimes (Rayleigh dipole below `x=0.1`, the Mie kernel on `[0.1, 50]`, the geometric opaque-sphere `Q_abs -> 1` above), the integral a log-spaced trapezoid over 128 grain sizes. The distribution is DATA: `slope`/`a_min`/`a_max` are arguments (the Dohnanyi -3.5 the reserved validation anchor for the upstream coagulation, never inlined); `(n, k)` and `rho` are per-composition data (the alien seam). Verified against the same integral over the f64 BHMIE: silicate-like (`m=1.68+0.03i`, `rho=3.3`, MRN `[0.005, 0.25]um`) gives `kappa_abs(0.5um)=2832`, `(10um)=74.5`, `(100um)=7.43 cm^2/g`, the far-IR `1/lambda` fall at constant index (the `lambda^-2` of real dust is the wavelength-dependent `k(lambda)`, not this constant-index kernel), and the EXACT reduction to the size-independent closed Rayleigh form at long wavelength. 5 tests, 318 physics total, pins hold. The BRUGGEMAN MIXING RULE LANDED byte-neutral: `civsim_physics::opacity::bruggeman_effective_index(fractions, indices)` derives the effective complex index of a grain built from several condensate species by the symmetric effective-medium rule `sum_i f_i (eps_i - eps_eff)/(eps_i + 2 eps_eff) = 0` (each `eps_i = (n_i + i k_i)^2`), solved by Newton (`f' = -3 sum f_i eps_i/(eps_i + 2 eps_eff)^2`) from the volume-weighted seed in the deterministic wide-fixed complex arithmetic, then `eps_eff -> (n, k)`. Composition is DATA: the fractions are the disposer condensate assemblage, each `(n, k)` a measured row (the alien seam). Scale-free in the fractions (the root is homogeneous in `f`), fail-loud. Verified against the exact two-component quadratic (sil+ice 50/50 -> n=1.4912, k=0.0144, matches to 6 digits), the pure-component reduction (returns its own index), and the monotone rise of the effective `k` with the metal (iron) fraction. 6 tests, 324 physics total, pins hold. So the generator's `optical constants x mixing rule x size distribution x Mie` chain is now built end to end (measured `(n,k)` rows -> Bruggeman mix -> `mie_q_abs` -> size-distribution integral -> `kappa_abs(lambda)`). Remaining arc steps (the 3c-iii integration): the disposer-condensate-fraction composition wire (feeds the fractions from the disposer output), the Lorentz-Drude estimator fallback for a condensate with no measured row, then the Rosseland assembly (the multi-species monochromatic total plus the gas floor, Rosseland-averaged) and the bounded T<->kappa midplane fixed point. The MELT-PHASE substrate (rung 0, the kernel's third phase type) LANDED byte-neutral in `civsim_physics::melting`, derived-in-form from each endmember's melting signature `(T_m, dH_fus, dV_fus)` with no fitted constant: the Schroeder-van Laar liquidus, the emergent binary eutectic (the crossing of two saturation curves, never authored), the lever-rule melt fraction over both primary fields, the complete-solid-solution loop (the other binary topology), the N-component multi-saturation solidus (`sum x_i = 1`, the eutectic generalized to an open data-driven assemblage), the Clapeyron pressure term (`dT_m/dP = dV_fus/dS_fus`, a thermodynamic identity so the measured melting curve is a self-check), and the adiabatic decompression melting column (`adiabatic_melt_column`) that pools the derived melt into crust. Rendered to an owner-facing map artifact (hypsometric terrain, the volcanic provinces, and a live drag-affected eruption). - DONE (Agent A, PR #141, MERGED to main; the owner's re-baseline nod given, the gate confirmed pins-on-record then merge): the **hydrology evaporation units-bug fix**, an independent correctness re-pin landing right after #143 (NOT subsumed into #143, whose runtime physicalization defers to the atmosphere arc; #141 lands the real evaporation flux NOW so the food web and B's productivity water term read a real flux rather than zero). The bug: `environ.rs step_hydrology` fed the ground `fluid.moisture_content` [0,1] into `evaporation_rate`'s `e_ambient` port (bound to `fluid.vapor_pressure` [MPa]), so the Dalton deficit `e_s - moisture` was always negative and evaporation was IDENTICALLY ZERO in every scenario. The derive-first fix: `e_ambient = moisture * e_saturation(T)` (the alpha-ET proxy), so the deficit `e_s * (1 - moisture)` is a proper vapour-pressure deficit scaling with dryness, no authored value.
